 The West Bengal Petroleum Dealers Association has called for a partial strike on November 3 and a full strike on November 15
 3 november ko petroleum dilers tel companiyon se kharidari nahin karenge jisase dopaher ko stock khatm hone par logon ko pareshaani ho sakati he
 After the nationwide strike call, the decision association says that they have to take these steps due to increasing cost of running petrol pumps and decreasing the cost
 ye kadam ol india petroleum dilers association(aipda) ke rashtravyapee hadtaal ke aahvaan ke tahat uthaaya gaya he
 On November 15, 3,000 West Bengal and 53,300 petrol pumps across the country will be on strike
 sarkaar ke saamne maangenwest bengal petroleum dilers association ke adhyaksh tushaar kanti sen ne kaha, 'ham bahut kam munaafe par kaam kar rahe hai, isse kharchon kaa puraa kar paanaa mushkil ho rahaa he
 Our business is currently at stake
 hamaari mukhya maang munafa badhaane kii he
 On November 3, we will not buy oil from oil companies
 vahiin 15 november ko na ham tel kharidenge or na hi bechenge
 This can cause problems to customers

 If these issues are not resolved then most of us may have to leave this business

 On November 15, all 3,000 petrol pumps in the state, including 180 in Kolkata, will remain closed
 bataa den ki petrol pump dilers ne 19 or 26 oktober ko shaam 7 baje se 15-15 minute kaa 'blassout' kiya tha
 His century partnership with Tillakaratne Dilshan's century and captain Mahela Jayawardene saw Sri Lanka equalize to 1–1 in the second match of the Best of Three Finals of the tri-odi series with an easy victory over Australia
 dilashaan ne 119 gend par 10 chaukon kii madad se 106 ran kii pari khilne ke alaava jayavardhane (80) ke saath pehle wicket ke liye 179 or kumaar sangakaara (naabad 51) ke saath 55 ran kii saajhedaari kii jisase srilanka ne 34 gend shesh rahete do wicket ganvaakar australia ke 272 ran ke lakshya ko hasil kar liya

 srilanka ko is samay jeet ke liye 11
 There was a need for 38 runs in 4 overs, which he scored easily

 Dinesh Chandimal remained unbeaten after scoring 17 runs
 isse pehle australia ko clark or warner ne visham paristhitiyon se ubaara

 vah lagaataar do vanade maichon main shatak jadne vaale aathven australian ballebaaj ban gayi hai
 Australia started off to bat after winning the toss and got off to a poor start

 1
 Before taking any remedy, it is most important that you brush well twice a day

 2

 3

 4

 5

 6
